country_event = { #Esperanto event
	id = 450007
	title = EVTNAME450007
	desc = EVTDESC450007
	picture = "jews"
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owns = 706 # Warsaw
		year = 1887
		civilized = yes
		invention = expressionist_literature
		literacy = 0.3 #Let's hope they know how to write before books
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 7 #26.7.1887, publication of the Unua Libro
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			month = 7
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA450007 #Adopt
		any_pop = {
			literacy = 0.01
		}
		prestige = 5
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB450007 #Discard
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_pop_culture = polish
					has_pop_culture = ashkenazi
				}
			}
			consciousness = 0.5
		}
		prestige = 5
	}
	
}
country_event = {
	id = 251000
	title = "The $COUNTRY_ADJ$ War of Independence"
	desc = "$DATE_LONG$ ($YEAR$)"
	major = yes
	picture = Riot
	is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
		name = "To Arms!"
		war = {
			target = FROM
			defender_goal = {
				casus_belli = annex_core_country
			}
			attacker_goal = {
				casus_belli = eu4_colony_asks_independence
			}
			call_ally = no
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = 250999
		}
	}
}

##251xxx ~ Colonial independence events
# Canada
country_event = {
 id = 251001
 title = EVTNAME251001
 desc = EVTDESC251001
 major = yes
 picture = Riot
 trigger = {
  is_independant = yes
  capital_scope = {
   OR = {
    continent = europe
    continent = asia
   }
  }
  NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_independence }
  has_global_flag = der_postcolonialism 
  is_possible_vassal = CAN
  NOT = { exists = CAN } 
 }
    mean_time_to_happen = {
  months = 120
  modifier = {
   factor = 10000
   NOT = { year = 1805 }
  }
  modifier = {
   factor = 0.75
   year = 1845
  }
  modifier = {
   factor = 0.75
   year = 1855
  }
  modifier = {
   factor = 0.75
   year = 1860
  }
  modifier = {
   factor = 0.5
   year = 1865
  }
 }
    immediate = {
  set_country_flag = CAN_independence
  any_owned = {
   limit = {
    is_core = CAN
   }
   secede_province = CAN
   remove_core = THIS
  }
  CAN = {
   leadership = 80
   years_of_research = 5
   set_country_flag = buro_independence
   election = yes
   any_owned = {
    fort = 1
   }
  }
 }
 option = {
  name = EVTOPTA251001
  create_vassal = CAN
  diplomatic_influence = {
   who = CAN
   value = 200
  }
  relation = {
   who = CAN
   value = 50
  }
  ai_chance = {
   factor = 25
  }
 }
    option = {
  name = EVTOPTB251001
  CAN = { country_event = { id = 251000 days = 1 }
  }
  relation = {
   who = CAN
   value = -50
  }
  ai_chance = {
   factor = 75
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.5
    badboy = 1 #25 infamy
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.75
    badboy = 0.5 #12.5 infamy
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 10000
    civilized = no
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 1.5
    crime_fighting = 0.75
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.5
    involved_in_crisis = yes #World tension
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.5
    government = democracy
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.5
    has_recently_lost_war = yes
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.5
    OR = {
     anarcho_liberal = 20
     socialist = 30
     communist = 30
    }
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 2
    OR = {
     reactionary = 30
     fascist = 30
    }
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 2
    is_cultural_union = yes
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.1
    is_disarmed = yes
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 2
    is_greater_power = yes
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 10000
    is_independant = no
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 3
    is_mobilised = yes
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 1.5
    is_secondary_power = yes
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.2
    lost_national = 0.1 #Lost at least 10% of national provinces
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 3
    military_spending = 0.75
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.2
    nationalvalue = nv_liberty
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 2
    nationalvalue = nv_order
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 10000
    national_provinces_occupied = 0.3
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 2
    num_of_cities = 50
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 10000
    num_of_revolts = 3
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.1
    NOT = { total_amount_of_divisions = 15 }
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.1
    NOT = { total_num_of_ports = 5 }
   }
   modifier = {
    factor = 0.5
    OR = {
     war = yes
     war_exhaustion = 10
    }
   }
  }
 }

#2611xx - Oceanian continent
#2612xx - African continent
#2613xx - African diaspora colonies
country_event = {  id = 261000  title = "EVTNAME261xxx"  desc = "EVTDESC261xxx"  picture = "census"    trigger = {   number_of_states = 1   has_country_flag = buro_independence    capital_scope = {    OR = {     continent = north_america     continent = south_america    }    OR = {     pop_majority_culture = amerikaner     pop_majority_culture = sudreicher     pop_majority_culture = north_german     pop_majority_culture = swiss     pop_majority_culture = south_german     pop_majority_culture = german    }   }   NOT = { has_country_flag = fixed_261 }  }    immediate = { set_country_flag = fixed_261 }    mean_time_to_happen = {   months = 1  }   option = {   name = "Amen."   primary_culture = amerikaner capital_scope = { assimilate = yes }	ai_chance = { factor = 100 }	}	option = {  	name = "(Player-only) What's wrong with the old tongue?"	capital_scope = { assimilate = yes }	ai_chance = 0	}}
